申報本埠增刊談言白山黑水  瓊聲　　素被我們騷客時人所謳歌讚美的（白山黑水）（東北），自從被敵人强姦公意的成立（王道政治）之後，對内對外總是自吹自捧的譽爲（樂士），（無苦無憂）的（新國　）　這樣的宣傳，令人聽了實在欣羨得很，因此我念要着着所謂，王道政治）所謂（樂士）所謂（新國家）到底是怎樣一回事？　　政治軍事經濟等的積極侵略，無容在此多贅，且擇其微末細節略舉一二，就可以（卽小見大）我卽以（三毒政策）略爲述論。三毒政策者何，卽對鴉片娼妓賭博之提倡與奬勵是也。查東北自（新國家）成立後·各地設鴉片公賣局，零賣所，日鮮浪人擁其前，剌刀大砲殿其後，是以最近東北人民，染芙蓉癖者，業已九百餘萬億，卽佔会人口三分之一之巨。每年吸土九千七百斤，共耗金錢數一千八百四十餘萬元。至賭博一事，完全公開，賓局會局等，徧及城村鄉鎭，而大連（俱樂部）資本之以幾十萬幾百萬日金開辦者，數以十計。各地會局寳局，迷惑人民至於敗家蕩產，失節自殺，更難枚數。至娼妓一事，（新國家）更體恤微情，免納營業稅，施行奬勵，因之妓館等，遍及鄉鎭。經濟破產生活維艱之中國婦女，竟以皮肉生涯，爲最佳之出路。而各烟館賭局之聘用（女招待），更使其佈滿黄帝子孫的女性。　　我們關内的許多（癮君子），好玩朋友，賭棍常常防有警察來打麻煩，也許這些情形會使他們感到（新國家）眞的成了（樂土）罷，然而我們不能不說是極痛心的事實。日本對於烟賭的不惜竭力擴充普及，不特在這上面可以歛取無數人民的金錢，而且具有消磨意志，和緩反抗的最大目的。而對於娼妓的奬勵，更一方面想使東北人民在性的享樂中消沉，一方面用以擴大對於東北婦女肉體上的蹂躪！　　（白山黑水）目前已經可說是由東北人民的白骨所砌成，血涙所浸漬，我知道了，所謂（王道政治），所謂新國家），所謂（樂土），原來如是。秋之街  張君　　深秋的薄暮。　　向晚的太陽光斜照在摩天樓頂·軟弱·帶點悲凉。街聲却趁了這時節擾攘起來！！　　（都會是夜的都會。）　　獨自在街上彳亍着：没有伴侣，也不帶根司的克，連烟也不點上一支地望望灰暗的天，有重霧似的把發亮的星子遮了起來。這時候，池車連成一長串，一條無比的大長蛇突然到了都會的心腹那麽地在街心移動着。　　我有點驚駭。我想：没有一條街是靜寂的嗎？　　於是我找着找着······　　街燈的光照着我，在我的脚步後面，拖了個修長的人影，一羣英國兵咭咕着過去了！前邊却有一個貴婦人不坐汽車地，拉着哈吧狗興冲冲地走過來，我忙躱開一旁讓着她。　　那邊是跑馬塲。　　這邊是：一間舞塲。　　舞塲過去了。　　（爵士音樂已嚮起來。）　　一家Ｒestanrnat。　　（火腿香從門隙裏飄了出來。）　　接着是一家照相館。　　（最紅的電影明星的照片陳列着。）　　·····走着，走着，我終於轉了彎。　　彎過去是一條靜寂的街了。我的脚步放慢下來，微笑着，（我究竟找到了！）那麽興奮地，哥侖布發現了新大陸似地，我吹起一支愉快的曲子。　　天色已經漸漸陰暗下來。　　年虹燈這裏是没有的。兩邊是牆，死寂，陰暗；只有一輛黄包車懶散地拉着過來。我想：如果我能永遠這樣地安靜下來，我該多麽快樂哪！　　可是，一輛汽車衝來了。　　啵丨丨啵·······　　啊，牠打碎了我的安靜！　　·······我又回轉到熱鬧的地方。　　男人們挺着的；女子笑着臉。紅的，綠的燈火；撩人的爵士；···一切一切都是剌激！　　（剌激？剌激？剌激？）　　都會是剌激的呵！　　一切都在最高的速率上變化着：舞塲閃着眼，飯店閃着眼，戲院閃着眼······。賣淫的女人的誘惑，狐步舞的誘惑，瑪琳黛德麗的誘惑······。　　（今兒上舞塲去吧！）有人說。　　有人說：（大光明映玉闕英雌哪！）　　有人說：（站在那街角的女人滿漂亮呢！）　　（所以：都會有那麽多賣肉的女人。有那麽多新建築的影戲院。那麽多的舞塲。······）　　可是我今天却不想上那裏去。

Page 19

我要安靜！　　街上是不安靜的。而且是賽冷的；不是麽，已經是深秋了呵。　　吹着十月尾的風。　　吹着色情的風。　　吹着世紀末的風的丨丨　　都會的秋天的街上呵丨南京路上底　人們  忘　桂花殘了  阿蘋　　膽瓶裏的桂花殘　，細小的花朶舖滿了書桌，憔悴地，像悲秋的女人。三五秃枝，挾着黄葉，從瓶口探望脫離牠的伴侣，惋惜的，像失戀的詩人。　　去年，桂花開放的時節，我買來一個赭色的膽瓶，一個殷紅的香爐。每天，彷彿虔禱她丈夫靈魂安息的老婦人一樣，我燃了一柱雲香，從那嬝嬝的烟霧中度過秋天的早晨。　　赭色的膽瓶始終空着，我不想插花。牠是個可怕的囚籠，我不忍眼見她摧殘了處女般的花朶。　　對街是家花舖，奶白漆的橱窗中，呆着，插着，彩色的花紥。開着窗，見她從纖潔的手指中减少，就注視着我的膽瓶，牠是空的。　　太陽從窗口溜了進來，雲香完了，我穿上秋大衣出門。　　走到對街，佇立在花舖子外面，那外國女子隔窗中投了個微笑的媚眼，又俯頭編織她的絨綫。手指是纖潔的，像那些買花的一樣。　　懷愛那染着寇丹的手指，輕微的推開了奶白漆的矮門。手指的主人放下了工作，授了我一束股紅的花，像寇丹一樣的可愛，又想起那赭色的膽瓶。　　贓着舖道上的方塊，把自家的脚尖兒凑着邊緣計算着，玩笑似的，到了我的工作塲所。殷紅的花束慷慨地插在壁爐上的金魚缸裏，自家兒尖指没有染過殷紅的寇丹。　　那赭色的膽瓶始終究空着，到第二個秋天。　　　一束桂花插進膽瓶的時候，在赭色的旁邊映着一雙染過寇丹的纖潔的手指；天指的主人俯到我的耳畔說：　　（爲愛花的人送花來了。）　　赭色的花瓶呆着，對於這意外的賜與。　　（我不愛）（供）花哩！）我回答。　　（我愛的！）像對街那個外國女人一樣，投了個微笑的媚眼。　　誰是這赭色花瓶的主人呢？　　桂花殘了，秋老了．殷紅的香爐中飄散着烟熖。　　赭色的膽瓶又空着，你等候着第三個秋天到來吧！　　注意着自家兒的手指，没有染過殷紅的寇丹。　　偶然飄一眼到對街去，奶白漆的橱窗中，花朶從纖潔的手指中减少。那個外國女人俯着頭編織她的絨綫。　　赭色的膽瓶是空的。　　你寂寞嗎，桂花殘了？玻璃櫃外  散嘉　　括着風，下着雨，没到六點鐘天就暗了。在馬路轉角玻璃櫃内的年紅燈隨着路燈亮了，照在那掛着的一隻隻肥大的鷄鴨和一條條的烤肉上，把那烤得紅紅的皮上加上与層青色的光彩。香味從櫃内溜了出來，散在人行道上。走過的人總得因了那陣陣的香味轉過頭去看看那些肉和鷄。　　從那邊踱過來一個十幾歲的小孩，聳着肩，兩只手緊緊的抱着胸，想减少一些風的刑罰。赤着足，拖着雙破鞋。褲子破得可以瞧見半個屁股。上衣没了領。頭髮長長的，臉兒瘦得像猴子。　　那孩子在那玻璃櫃外站下了。年紅燈的青色光映在他的臉上，越發使他不成個人樣。他拉拉破衣角。眼睛直挺挺的瞧着那鷄那肉。嘴内的水分突然增加起來，差不多要滿出來了，於是他拚命向喉嚨裏嚥，但越嚥越多。終於他把髒極的袖拭了拭嘴唇。　　掛在店裏面的鐘鐺鐺地響了六下，那馨音驚動了呆立着的小伙子。（是吃夜飯的時候了呵！）他想。抬起頭來望了望黑沉沉的天，再用手抹了抹嘴唇。掛在櫃内的鷄和肉的引誘力更大了，香味也更濃厚了。他瞧着那肥美的食物，肚子咕咕地響了。下意識地用手按了按腹部，解開那褲帶，又把牠重新緊緊地繫了起來。　　（二毛錢拆燒！）一個顧客把雙毫丢在砧板上，店裏的伙計從玻璃櫃内拿下一條肉，切作一片征地，包好了交給那個顧客，顧客走了，伙計在砧板上發現了一些肉屑，用刀一括，都扔在地上。　　櫃外的小伙子用舌砸了砸唇，暗嘆息。（爲什麽我連一些肉屑都没有得吃呢？）他懷疑了。他瞧瞧人家，又看看自己。可不是一樣有嘴巴有肚子的麽？　　脚有些累了，輕輕地斜倚在玻璃櫃上。肉和鷄跟他只隔開一層玻璃呵。（要是没玻璃的話······）他想。　　（丢那媽！）櫃内的伙計睜着眼駡了。他連忙挺直了身體，彳亍地走了過去。再用袖管擦了擦嘴，便消失在人叢中了。　　香味依舊散在人行道上，鷄那，那肉·······時節的心  仃　　秋：秋的景色，秋的夜月，秋的晚星，秋的寒風，秋的情調，秋是一個充滿着憂鬱的季節。秋是那麽苦悶的啊！　　秋的心是凄凉的，秋的眼睛是多情的，秋的面龐是悲愁的，秋的聲音是悽慘的，秋的嘴髻是蒼白的，秋的容顏是那麽抑鬱不樂的呀！秋，秋，使人掀動心情的秋，使人回憶過去的秋，使人沉湎於萬種愁思留戀愛人追懷故物的秋。秋好像是個失戀的女子。　　春天是個年輕的女郎，她有的是活潑，生躍躍的，充滿着朝氣的力量，充滿着奮發的現象，美麗的，健康的，可愛的，使人感覺生生之欲的！不像秋天那樣。　　夏天是個及時的少女，她有的是熱情，火辣辣的，充滿着希望，幻像，金色的好夢。她使人感覺生的必要，長進的愉快，一切都是暖熱的激動，奮發的，向前邁步的那種氣槪。不像秋天那樣。不像春天那樣。是十足十的夏天自己那樣。　　冬天是個嚴肅的寡婦，她有的是暮氣，陰没沉的，衰頽頽的，充滿着，殘年的痛苦，充滿着老大莊嚴，充滿着緊漲的危急，充滿着難堪的，薄情的，冷酷的，缺少友誼的熱情。冬天過於單純，過於蕭煞，過於萎縮，過於使人感覺終結的楚痛。冬天不是春天那樣，不是秋天那樣，又不是像夏天那樣。　　我不高興夏天，我不喜歡冬天，我不贊成春天，我也不留戀秋天啊！我願意，是春夏秋冬四季都有，那種混合天氣。　　可是，這是多麽不幸的呀，我這一顆的心，抱着希罕的情懷，追慕着不可能的現象，心是熱的，氣是旺的，力是足的，幻想的魔術是無窮的。　　然而，這一顆心呀！這顆捉摸不定的心，這顆創傷的心，這顆充溢着無邊無際的心，是苦，是酸，是甜，是辣，是冷，是熱，是黑，是白，是無底的，是不可訴說的心情啊！　　我這一顆的心呀，我這希求的一種氣候呀，我這盼望的一位女郎呀！幾時能够實現？幾時能够消除了我心中的煩燥？幾時能够使我踏上人生的樂土？幾時能够·····？　　心的呼喚，情的奔動，血的泉湧，涙的汹流，生的呐喊，死的呻吟，挣扎，鬥爭，變幻無窮的世事和我這一顆幻滅的心。業餘信箱合法商號均受保護編者先生：　　我有一位本家叔叔經商美國，已有十餘載，六年前返國，在鄉下市鎭，合股開設一銀號，由吾叔任經理之職，年來已獲利二萬餘元。最近因環境影響，突起風潮，所有活期存欵，和定期欵項，一律爭來提欵。該號一時不能應付，遂暫停營業。正當失敗，本無痛苦可言。惟最令人憤慨者，有一股東，欲奪經理之職，用毒辣手段，恣意摧殘，横加壓迫，限吾叔於最短期間，將他未到期之長期存欵交出，否則要將吾叔全家殺害。現該號已於月前復業，所有活期及長期欵項，均已清還。惟該銀號未在政府註册，對於破壞名譽及恐嚇之詞，可否訴之於法院？用何方法可以控訴？尚祈從速指示爲盼。敬上，並頌撰安。　　康業上　　編者按：康業君來函係抽象形容，殊難以具體方案答覆。但該人旣有欵存於錢莊，自然可以提回。如實有破壞名譽，或以生命財產相恐嚇，而危及公安者，可依法控訴，並應隨時報告本地警務機關，注意。　　至於商店未經註册，其店號苟非被故意侵害，似難求法律保障：惟並通一船問題，如營業，財產等則均享有法律上保護之權利，此與未經註册無關。　　啟事　昨日談言手腕的運用誤運（動），特此更正。　增刋編輯室

自我職業介紹　　　雪女十；浙江平縣籍，現年十八　　曾於初中兼華文打字梭畢業，現願任機關練習生打字員書記等職，月薪不計，如需此項人材者希投函北浙江路六桂坊六號楊女士收轉。　　薛君，北平人，年二十五，曾在高中卒業，操國語非常流利，今願担任家庭敎授及公司洋行等處職務，如有需用上項人材者，請函閘北刑家橋路一七九號。無綫電播音莭目歌唱　　敦本（八○○）　　玫瑰圖　下午五時至六時　　寄生草（前奏）好朋友來了（周恭張如）吾捨不得你（曼娜）特别快車（吳芳）粉紅色的夢（曼麗）吾的愛人就是你（楊曾恕張如）藍雙飛（玲玲）娘子軍（曼娜）新戀（曼麗）　　中西（一○四○）　　都會社　下午五時三刻至六時半　　Ｗlustiag　in　the　danp（前奏曲）娘子軍（姚秀雲綠裙隊喻義薛硯）航空救國（傳瑞英）萬里尋兄（姚秀雲）愛情是什麽（薛硯慈）母搖燕曲（傅瑞英）　　東方（一○二○）　　妙音團下午六時十分至七時　　昭君怨（前奏曲）好朋友來了（張雪沙）給摩登小姐（羅鶯）擱樓上小姐（黄韵）别矣巴黎（張仙琳）哥哥愛我嗎（張雪沙）特别快車（馬陋芬）花生米（張仙琳）　　敦本（八○○）　　玫瑰團　下午七時至八時　　平湖引子（前奏）柴羅蘭（曼娜）你要那個抱（曼麗）小妹妹的心（吳芳）吾不致忘記你（張如）花弄影（玲玲）戀愛的滋味（曼娜）龍翔鳳舞（曼麗）國花（張如）　　安定（八六○）　　芙蓉團　下午七時至八時　　前奏曲（全體）永遠在後臺（雪芬）永别了弟弟（雪雪）再見吧故鄉（露茜）人面桃花（雪華）風雨琴歌（雪雪）别矣巴黎（徐文璧）漁光曲（露茜）　　華東（一三六○）　　妙音團　下午八時至九時　　西宫詞（鋼琴獨奏）安慰（張仙琳）悲秋（羅鶯）戀愛經（馬陋芬黄韵）昭君怨（張雪沙）慈母搖籃曲（馬陋芬）夜半的私語（黄韵）夢中情人（張仙琳）　　中西（一○四○）　　玫瑰團　下午八時三刻至九時四十分　　樂哉樂哉（前奏）春江花月夜（張如）再見吧故鄉（曼麗）鴛鴦怨（曼娜）新戀（張如）人生幾回逢（曼麗）瞎子算命（玲玲）三蝴蝶（吳芳）　　國華（一二○○）　　大都會　下午九時至十埘　　進行曲（全體）小妹妹不要哭（雪芬）航空救國（包雪雪）情伴（雪琴流朗）思量（雪華）廣州小姐（露茜）漁公樂（雪芬）燕雙飛（雪琴）永遠在後臺（雪華）　　利利（一二四○）　　妙音團　下午十時至十一時　　可愛的春天（前奏曲）夜來香（羅鶯）夜半的私語（黄韵）可憐的秋香（張雪沙）宫璇艶史（張仙琳）贊美勇士曲（黄韵）　　安定（八六○）　　玫瑰團　下午十時至十一時　　老三六（前奏）木蘭詞（曼娜）杏花天（曼娜）麻雀和小孩（吳芳玲玲張如）吾怎麽捨得你（曼麗）愛神的箭（張如）彈詞　　中西（一○四○）　　姚小菴龐學師·珍　塔　上午十時至十一時·······　　開篇（勸世）　　　　花謝　多紅。　　秉畢若　中　一業浮萍　大海。人生何處不相逢。石　當。范丹窮。　發甘露　太公。彭祖壽高八　歲。顏回短命太明聰。也不是天不公來地不公。總是那得失榮華經命官。奉勸世人休碌碌。爭名奪利一塲空。得逍遥處且歡娱。遇情陶樂酒九盅。惡覇行凶多是假。可曾見過楚重　。萬丈維敵英雄將。只落得自刎烏烏一旦空。韓信功勞稱十丈。後來身喪未央宫。豈非多在夢魂中。　　航運電台（一一八○）　　張夢飛禪詞　下午一時至一時三刻　　開篇　御碑亭孟月華避雨　　月華是夕陽影憂走匆匆。誰知曉驀地空中竟起疾風。一利那颯颯蕭蕭吹漸烈。到後來黄塵匝地捲長空。眼見那兒童斷了風爭綫。霎時無影又無蹤。耳聽得道旁樹木沙沙嚮。那風是入竹穿林勢吏兇。吹得那逆水扁舟忙靠岸。吹得那順風歸掉掛孤邊。吹得那長條柳葉眠還起。吹得那無力楊花西復東。况且是烏雲頃刻把天遮蔽。景色依稀與薄暮同。猛聽得黨靈當頭心胆碎。却原來雷聲不住嚮隆隆。電光是萬道金蛇在空際舞。宛如天半掛長虹。分明是雨師風伯來相會。所以敎雷公電母做先錄。這時候一片平原人迹少。孟月華難禁小鹿撞心胸。况且是凉生衣袂春寒嫩。猛抬頭細雨濕濛濛。但只見行人都避雨回家去。月華是幾度籌思計己窮。體軟如綿蕪氣力。数人兒怎不怨蒼穹。然而是巧合天緣從古說。那月華避雨向亭中。偏與書生陌路逢。話劇　　中西（一○四○）　　觀音社（兒女英雄傳）下午七時一刻至八時　　兩個强盜，名字是韓七跟李七，一直護送他們到淮安，只把牲口收回了，安公子贈銀！他們並没接受，於是告别了！　　安公子的大事辦好，把經過的情形告訴了家裏如此，不是都很滿意的嗎！我可以贈給他們一句祝詞：（皆大歡喜！）　　華興（一二六○）　　觀音社（紅樓夢丨大鬧寗國府）下午八時一刻至九時　　現在熙鳳，這所謂醋缸出世了！這一點就可以　明白知道了，尤二姐所以會也弄得一個哀的結果，這不用說一定是爲這一缸醋的關係？但故事没有這樣的簡單，他們還要大鬧一下，這寗國府哩！好，這裏頭，别提了可以說一句（熱鬧非常了）　　永生（一○八○）　　觀音社（好青年）　下午九時至十時　　三個臭皮匠，合成諸葛亮，不錯！的確不錯的！現在陸敬巧娘頡云竟會聯合着回文娟進攻了唉！足智多謀的同占幗英雄萬文娟届此也有難爲底麽付之困難誕生了！　　華美（一○六○）　　（啼笑因緣）下午十時至十一時　　秀姑惹下了禍端，還不逃之夭夭嗎？除非是儍子才不走！和尚們發現了將軍高臥到嚮午尚不響，這才看看一如董卓股底死肥豬原來還躺的那兒了！哈！　　壁上留的一首詩，和尚們方知道所謂一不平女子者，原來就是她呀！　　秃驢們不約而同的喊了一聲：（我的媽呀！）　　新聲（一三八○）　　民生社（雪盃圓）　下午十時至十一時　　負義，投靠，僅盃，搜查，逃生，捉莫。更動節目　　市音（一三四○）　　上午九時半至十時半　唱片　　十時半至十一時半　沈章慈開篇　　十一時半至十二時半　肩雅　徐文壁開篇　　下午十二時半至一時半　古今團話劇　　一時半至　時半　朱寳興四明文書　　二時半至三時　周雅廬徐文璧開篇　　三時至四時　楊斌金楊振雄描金鳳　　四時至五時　江笑笑滑稽　　　五時至六時　周血血滑稽　　六時至七時　劉春山滑稽　　七時至八時　陳瑞麟陳雪麟琴珠塔　　八時至十時　顧雷音話劇　　十時至十一時　莊海泉蘇灘　　十一時至十二時　商情報告　　十二時至一時　徐哲身福爾摩斯　　一時至二時　徐哲身濟公傳

申報本埠增刊　汽車周刊一九三五年式比利拉新車槪述  篔　　經濟合算一大特色　　飛霞廠精造。一九三五年式比利拉新車。茲已由本埠經售商。大利汽車行。運抵此間。連日汽車界人士。紛往參觀。無不大加讚賞。嘆爲驚人傑搆。新車優點。不勝枚舉。茲特略述大槪。以餉讀者。　　經濟合算。要爲比利拉新車最顯著之特色。按當舉世不景氣之今日。一般汽車購主。對於車輛之購置。自無不以經濟爲前提。比利拉新車。蓋卽爲適合此種需要。而悉心創製者。據實地試騐。比利拉載客五人以疾駛。計每一加侖汽油。足可行三十六英里。以本市車務情形而言。蓋正需要此種車輛也。新車又一特色。厥爲特别寬敞舒適是也。若同樣尺寸之其餘各種車輛。如儎客五人。仍甚寬暢適意。則在經濟方面。必不免有所犧牲。但比利拉則有異於斯。考其所以然者。蓋以四門不用柱子。自可增加地位。使置身其中者。倍覺寬敞。彌感安適也。　　車身外觀壯麗。漆飾絕佳。更以採用飛機動力化原理。故尤美妙動人。前座靈活。便於調整。車身製以純鋼。安全之至。新車輪距。較去年式樣加長三寸。車身地位因而愈增。其穏適亦愈甚。至於内部。旣極富麗。且殊經濟。全部地位。雖一寸一分。皆盡量利用。無一虚耗。所有各項表盤。完全集中裝置於一六寸經之大表盤上。羅羅清疏。瞭如指掌。墊靠製以特優質料。經久耐用。開關近在手邊。極便運用。至於引擎。與上年式樣相較。僅小有差别。其最關重要者。計爲自動發動機。赤久諧動。及四擋齒輪盤等。　　芝加哥之史丹脱及麥廸遜街。係世界上最熱閙之一角。今有人在該地打「落袋」。當係歷史上第一次。圖為一輛一九三四年新司蒂倍克廸克推多號轎車。上載一只十足尺寸之白朗維克彈子台。時彈子大王Ｗillie　Hoppe正與美國彈子恊會會長C.A.Storer比賽之情形。地上飛又得錦標  敷　　阿爾帕山競賽獲勝　　赫德森汽車公司推銷部經理阿卜特氏。頃接報告。日前舉行之阿爾帕山競賽。勝利錦標。首相冰山杯。爲李查遜君所獲得。所駕之汽車。則赫德森出品地上飛也。同時臺維斯君。駕另一地上飛。參加競賽。竟與李氏並駕齊驅。無分伯仲。因亦獲奬同樣冰山杯焉。按李台二君。均爲業餘汽車家。並百汽車競賽職業專家。而阿爾帕山路。且從未駕車經過。乃竟一鳴驚人。有此成績。故尤覺難能可貴。而地上飛之精優卓絕。亦因而愈爲人所信服。攀拿阿爾帕山競賽。早經一般人公認爲歐洲境内一切汽車競賽中之最艱險者。蓋此項競賽。包括必須攀登之歐洲最高山路廿三處。及須儘六日内。行畢一千七百五十英里。而此項哩程。其中位於裘戈斯拉夫。及奥斯特利亞境内之數百里。且極崎嶇狹隘峻險之至。車行其間。頗有行不得也之嘆。全程係由尼斯起。朝北經班苗，印特萊坑，聖慕禮寺，轉向東南。經意大利境阿爾帕山。直達威尼斯海岸。然後朝東經阜姆及薩格勒勃。折而西北行。經慕尼墟之山區。而到達終點。綜計沿途經過六國。加入競賽之汽車。共計四十有五輛。汽車瀛談  沛　　美國大盗頌揚福特速率超羣　　狄林傑是美國最近的一個劇盗。本年七月二十二日被警務人員在支加哥將他生生格斃。不過他的大名。已經轟動了全美國的男男女女。大家都當他是一個極神秘的大盗。他的事蹟。差不多全給人家作談話的資料了。他生前最大的絶技。就是搶刦銀行和越獄。忽而打家刦舍。忽而穿墻兎脱。神岀鬼没。弄得州警無法可想。後來終究天網恢恢。飲彈伏法。也是一件大快人心的事。這里還有他生前寫給汽車大王福特的一封信。現在在地屈洛傳為佳話。狄林傑的信説。「親愛的福特先生。我要謝謝你製造出這樣的出色的汽車。要是我被捕的話。那末拘我的人。也一定是坐福特車的了。約翰狄林傑（簽字））這封信是福特在七月十七日所收到的。起初以爲是有人有意開玩笑。直到狄林傑伏法之後。經警署人員騐對筆蹟。方始曉得這信眞是大盜的親筆哩。這封信是從明納巴立土（米内沙太）所發的。而那時所得報告。都說狄林傑藏匿在伊里諾·印第安那和米西根等地。至於狄林傑之所以稱頌福特者。實因他曾利用福特。脫逃出幾次很危險的塲合。最著名的是在印第阿納的克郎嘴地方。他用一枝木造的假槍脫離樊籠。　　克雷斯勒汽車已届一百萬輛　　著名克雷斯勒汽車。在最近的七年之中。已經造到第一百萬輛的汽車了。這一件事也是美國汽車界中深堪注意的。因爲要在這樣短暫的時期中。完成一百萬輛汽車。實在是件很不容易的事哩。我們試看整個的汽車界。他們的造車成績究竟怎樣。在一九零零年眞正的汽車工業方纔開始。十二年之久中。整個的汽車界方始完成最初的第一百萬輛汽車。據紀錄上的登載。那時候所有的汽車無不包括在内。一九二八年時克雷斯勒潑萊茅斯開始登塲。嗣後便獲得很鞏固卓越的地位。一九三一年時浮力引擎架發明應用。那時候克雷斯勒在汽車界中。便一躍而至第三位了。這個地位至今没有衰落。第一百萬輛的克雷斯勒潑萊茅斯出廠的時候。廠中的執行人員和許多市民都參加儀禮。克雷斯勒氏親自脫去了長服。駕了那輛汽車出來。廠工們都向他歡迎。克雷斯勒氏向報界人員說。（我相信現在大衆所獲得的汽車價值。是從來汽車歷史中的最鉅大的了。今後數年中低級車的式樣機構都不至有顯著的更動。而我更相信未來的低價汽車。還要漂亮。近代化和格外經濟。不過總還保存着原有的式樣。至於進步方面。我們可以無庸顧慮。汽車事業是一直前進着。對於社會和經濟方面的進展。像和已往的一樣）云云。　　英國汽車鳴角　統制區域展大　　英國的汽車。現在有）定的時間不能亂撳喇叭。所以汽車鳴角無形中已受到一種統制了。這一點在倫敦已經有相當時期的試騐。很有成效。所以運輸部長現在已經通令全國。凡是人烟稠密的地方。都要施行這種統制。像倫敦一樣。這種禁令。在當初頒佈之後。已經獲得千萬封的謝信。禁止鳴角的時間爲下午十一時半起到次晨七時爲止。在這個時間當中。任何車輛。不得亂撳喇叭。違者罰英金兩鎊。這個（靜狀線）施行的條例。係從九月十六日起開始。事前舉行一種運動。利用報紙和無線電的播音。使得

1934.10.24

Chiang Kai-shek Arrives in Bian via Zheng 1

Received Jiang Bocheng and Others in Zheng

Inspected Welcoming Troops in Bian

(Kaifeng) Chairman Chiang's special train departed Zhengdong at 12:00 noon and arrived in Bian at 1:30 PM. Provincial government commissioners, heads of departments, military officers, and school representatives all welcomed him at the station. The route was heavily guarded by military police. Five minutes after the train arrived, Chairman Chiang stepped off to the sounds of military music and greeted the welcoming party. He then inspected the welcoming troops with Chairman Liu before returning to the train to rest. Madame Chiang, accompanied by Chairman Liu and his wife, traveled by car to the provincial government for a meal. Chiang disembarked at 4:00 PM to enter the city. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Zhengzhou) Chairman Chiang, accompanied by Madame Soong Mei-ling and Yang Yongtai, departed from Shaanxi on a special train on the morning of the 22nd and arrived in Luoyang. On the morning of the 23rd, at 8:00 AM, he arrived in Zhengzhou by special train from Luoyang. Liu Zhi, Jiang Bocheng, Hong Ludong, and other military and political leaders of Zhengzhou, numbering approximately a thousand, welcomed him at the station. He summoned Liu, Jiang, Hong, and others for instructions and inspected the progress of the New Life Movement in Zhengzhou. He then departed Zhengzhou by special train for Bian at approximately 12:00 noon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Kaifeng) Chairman Chiang arrived in Bian at 1:30 PM. Secretary-General Yang Yongtai accompanied him. Yang told the Central News Agency reporter that Chairman Chiang had an excellent impression of his inspection of the Northwest. Shaanxi and Gansu have made significant progress in construction. Bandits are gradually being suppressed, and the local area is very peaceful. He will stay in Bian for about one day. Whether he will go to Hankou or Nanjing has not yet been decided. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Hankou) Chairman Chiang stopped in Zhengzhou on the 22nd and only arrived in Bian on the 23rd. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

The requests from merchants are not something the Ministry of Finance can consider. As for unregistered banks, since they are not registered, there is no way to investigate, and their business scope is unlimited. The Ministry of Finance has long intended to take measures to ban them, but there are many privately-run banks that are not registered. Since the Ministry of Finance has not been able to order them to register one by one, it will resolutely ban them strictly in the future to avoid harming the public. Legislative Yuan Continues to Discuss the Special Part of the Criminal Law 8

Six Chapters Passed in Total, Morning and Afternoon

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held a general meeting on the morning of the 23rd to continue deliberating the draft revision of the Criminal Law. More than sixty committee members attended. Chairman Sun Fo announced the meeting and discussed Chapter Seven, Crimes Against Public Order. Articles 147, 148, 148, 150, 151, and 152 were all passed at the second reading without objection. Article 153 (Inciting soldiers not to perform their duties, or to disobey discipline, or to desert, shall be punished by imprisonment for not less than six months and not more than five years) and Article 154 (Those who recruit troops, issue military supplies, or lead troops without permission shall be punished by imprisonment for not more than five years). He Sui said that these two articles are more serious than Article 152, which punishes those who form a society for the purpose of committing crimes with imprisonment for not more than three years, and ringleaders with imprisonment for not more than seven years. The sentences for Articles 153 and 154 should both be changed to imprisonment for not less than one year and not more than seven years. Luo Ding, Zhu Hezhong, Sheng Zhenwei, and others advocated maintaining the draft revision, because the above two articles refer to the general population and not to soldiers, and Article 154 increases the penalty by two years compared to Article 164 of the current law. The chairman then put it to a vote. Of the 62 committee members present, only 19 supported increasing the penalties in Articles 153 and 154. The second reading was passed as per the draft revision. Articles 155, 156, and 157 were passed without objection. Article 158 (Whoever publicly damages, removes, or insults the national flag and national emblem of the Republic of China with the intent to insult the Republic of China shall be punished by imprisonment for not more than one year, detention, or a fine of not more than 300 yuan). Huang Youchang said that this article is listed according to Article 167 of the current law and is based on the order of the National Government on June 27, 1939. If there is an intent to insult the national flag and national emblem or the portrait of the Premier, they should be punished, and the degree of punishment should be stipulated in the criminal law. However, the article fails to include the meaning of the Premier's portrait, which is inconsistent with the National Government's order of the 18th year and the preamble of the draft constitution recently passed by the Legislative Yuan in the third reading, which marks the significance of Mr. Sun's teachings. Therefore, he advocated adding a paragraph to this article that those who intend to insult the Premier's teachings should also be punished. Zhao Chen said that this issue was discussed by the Criminal Law Committee when drafting the draft revision of the criminal law, because Article 241 states that public insults in public places of commemoration are punishable by imprisonment for not more than six months. Public places of commemoration include the meaning of the Premier's portrait. Sheng Zhenwei said that Huang's proposal is very good and can be included in Chapter 35, Crimes of Destruction and Damage. Zhu Hezhong, Deng Hongye, and others seconded Huang's intention. Wang Shufang said that regarding the insult of the Premier's portrait, a separate article should be listed to show respect for the Premier. After the discussion, the chairman put it to a vote. Of the 64 committee members present, 40 supported adding a separate article, and it was passed. Shi Weihuan said that in the new article, the words "Premier" should be changed to "Mr. Sun" according to the wording of the constitutional draft preamble, and the chairman designated the Criminal Law Committee to draft the article. Jian Youwen said that this chapter is Article 158 of Crimes Against Public Order, but it has no major relationship with this chapter. The chairman said that this is determined in imitation of European and American laws, because it is based on the patriotism of the people. If someone insults the national flag and is witnessed by others, they will be beaten by everyone, causing great chaos, so it should be included in this chapter. Next, Chapter Eight, Crimes of Escape, was discussed. There was no objection to Article 159. Clause 5 of Article 160 stipulates that if relatives within the fifth degree of consanguinity or the third degree of affinity of the spouse commit the crime of facilitating escape, the punishment may be mitigated. Zhong Tianxin said that Chinese people do not value the concept of the country as much as they value the concept of family. Such a provision seems to encourage Chinese people to attach more importance to the concept of family, so he advocated deleting Clause 5. Huang Youchang said that Clause 5 is newly included in the draft revision, and the scope of defining the fifth-degree of consanguinity and the third-degree of affinity is too broad. Please change it to the fourth-degree and the second-degree. Then, Lin Bin, Luo Ding, Zhao Chen, Chen Changheng, Shi Shangkuan, and others debated the crime of facilitating the escape of various relatives for a long time. The chairman put it to a vote, and the majority of committee members supported maintaining the draft revision. The second reading was passed. Article 161 and Chapter Nine, Crimes of Hiding Criminals and Destroying Evidence, Articles 162, 163, 164, and 165 were all passed in the second reading without objection. In Chapter Ten, Crimes of Perjury and False Accusation, Articles 166, 167, 168, and 169 were passed in the second reading. Later, Dai Xiujun said that in the current law, those who intend to harm direct relatives and commit crimes such as false accusations are subject to an increase of one-half of the original punishment, and those who intend to preserve their own or their relatives' freedom and reputation and make false statements about matters of important relationship to the case before or after the oath of witnesses, appraisers, and interpreters in court trials or when the prosecutor investigates, are exempt from punishment. The draft revision deleted them all. I don't know what the intention is. Liu Kejun, Luo Ding, and others said that no matter who they are, all false accusations infringe on the country's trial power and hinder the exercise of judicial power, and should be punished uniformly. The punishment cannot be increased by one-half for those who intend to harm direct relatives and commit the crime of the previous article, or exempt from punishment for the purpose of preserving their own or their relatives' freedom and reputation. Zhu Hezhong, Lu Zhiyi, Cheng Zhonghang, and others said that if the punishment is not increased for those who intend to harm direct relatives and commit crimes such as false accusations, it will have a great impact on society. If a son can falsely accuse his father, is it not different from animals? Moreover, it is not consistent with the spirit of Article 62 of the draft revision of the criminal law, which stipulates that those under the age of 18 who murder direct relatives shall be sentenced to death. Therefore, Article 181 and other articles should be restored to show the virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, righteousness, faith, love, and peace in our country. Lin Bin said that punishment should be based on the general public as the standard and on the country, not on kinship. It should only be asked whether the false accusation should be punished. It is not appropriate for a father to falsely accuse his son, or a son to falsely accuse his father, in human relationships. Even if it does, there is no damage to the falsely accused person, and the hindrance to the exercise of judicial power is greater, so punishment should be imposed uniformly according to law. Tao Lüqian, Chen Ruxuan, Gu Zhenggang, and others then spoke, all advocating that Article 181, Paragraph 1 of the current law should be restored. Chen Ruxuan even advocated that Article 183 should also be restored. After the discussion, the chairman put it to a vote. Of the 63 committee members in the room, only 30 raised their hands to support adopting the original meaning of Article 181, Paragraph 1. Some committee members then requested a counter-vote or a re-vote. The chairman then decided to use the standing vote method. Of the 63 committee members in the room, 32 stood up in support of adopting Article 181. Because it was the majority, it was passed and handed over to the Criminal Law Committee to reorganize the article. Only a few supported the restoration of Article 183, and it was not passed. Then, Secretary Tang Shiwei read out the various articles in Chapter Eleven, Crimes of Endangering Public Safety. The chairman announced the adjournment because it was already 12:00 noon and scheduled to continue the discussion in the afternoon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held a meeting at 4:00 PM on the 23rd to continue deliberating Chapter Eleven of the draft revision of the Criminal Law, Crimes of Endangering Public Safety. Except for Articles 170, 171, 180, and 181, the words (aircraft) were added under (boat and vehicle) in Paragraph 1, and the words (all) were added above (buildings) under (others) in Article 171, Paragraph 1. The words (daily use) were deleted in Article 191. The remainder was passed in the second reading according to the draft revision. Next, Chapter Twelve, Crimes of Counterfeiting Currency, was deliberated. Except for the deletion of Paragraph 2 of Article 195 and the revision of Paragraph 3 to (Attempted crimes in the preceding paragraph shall be punished), the remainder was passed according to the draft revision. After the chapter was discussed, the chairman announced the adjournment because it was already 6:30 PM and scheduled to continue the discussion on the afternoon of the 24th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

Japanese Building Roads in Jehol, Two Have Been Completed 11

Zhang Xueliang Speaks Freely of His Western Journey After Arriving in Hankou 12

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang met with reporters on the 23rd to freely speak of his thoughts on his western journey and his intentions to develop the Northwest, saying approximately that he accompanied Chairman Chiang to Luoyang, then to Xi'an, Lanzhou, and Ningxia for inspection. Chiang arrived in Kaifeng on the 23rd, and he flew to Hankou one day earlier. After traveling to various provinces, he realized the greatness of the Northwest. He saw the Great Wall of 10,000 miles built by Zuo Zongtang from Tongguan to Xinjiang and the ancient buildings of the Qin Canal and Tang Canal. Unfortunately, the trees protecting the roads were mostly destroyed. He deeply felt that our construction spirit is not only inferior to that of the ancestors of the remote era, but also far different from modern times, and is further destroyed, which is very distressing. Lanzhou has a woolen mill and an iron bridge, which are grand in scale. Ningxia leans against the Helan Mountains in the north and overlooks the Yellow River in the south. The situation is even more magnificent and is truly a military stronghold, but the soil is barren and the people are poor, not as well as Shaanxi and Gansu. He believes that the first thing to develop the West is to develop transportation. Fortunately, the Longhai Railway has been connected to Weinan and will be open to traffic by the end of the year to Xi'an on New Year's Day next year. The Shaanxi-Lanzhou Highway has also been completed and opened to traffic by the Economic Committee. However, this is only the first step and needs to be continued to be developed. He hopes that the people of the country will pay close attention and jointly seek development. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

繞行機場一匝 13

Traversing the Airfield Once

史考特擬對衆發言、但其聲爲歡呼所掩、二人因缺睡眠、皆甚疲乏、未幾、共乘一汽車繞行塲中、受衆歡呼、此後墨爾缽市長及飛行競賽發起人墨克斐生勞勃生等予以正式歡迎、民衆先唱（渠乃良友）歌、市長致歡迎詞

Scott intended to speak to the crowd, but his voice was drowned out by the cheers. Both men were very tired due to lack of sleep. Soon after, they rode together in a car, circling the airfield, receiving cheers from the crowd. Afterwards, the Mayor of Melbourne and the founder of the air race, Macpherson Robertson, and others gave them a formal welcome. The crowd first sang the song "He's a Jolly Good Fellow," and the Mayor delivered a welcoming speech.

市長繼致歡迎詞曰、（君等成績、乃英帝國青年之敎訓、示以造成英帝國之偉大特性、今猶存在）云、史考特答稱、（吾人頃以飛機爲慮、愈近墨爾缽、吾人之惶慮愈甚、神經剌激頗甚、余不能多言、故請白拉克致詞）云、白拉克乃走近放聲機前曰、（余終身未曾演說、余今所能言者、爲多謝諸君耳）、荷蘭領事趨前與英飛行家相見、代表荷蘭航空界贈以鮮花、史考特語路透訪員、（途中未嘗稍有睡眠、無時不愼重將事、但現覺安適、承此間人士予以盛大歡迎、吾人實深感謝）云、

The Mayor continued his welcoming speech, saying, "Your achievements are a lesson for the youth of the British Empire, demonstrating that the great characteristics that built the British Empire still exist." Scott replied, "We were worried about the plane, and the closer we got to Melbourne, the more worried we became. The nervous stimulation was quite intense. I cannot say much, so I will ask Black to say a few words." Black then walked to the microphone and said, "I have never given a speech in my life. All I can say now is thank you all." The Dutch Consul stepped forward to meet the English aviators and presented flowers on behalf of the Dutch aviation community. Scott told a Reuters reporter, "I haven't had any sleep along the way. I have been cautious about everything, but now I feel comfortable. We are deeply grateful for the grand welcome given by the people here."

勝利終屬英國

Victory Ultimately Belongs to Britain

競賽委員會副主席柯爾謂史白所表示之勇氣毅力决心、及其航空之技能、爲航空史中所僅見、其所駕者爲英製之飛機、而推動此飛機者、又爲英製之引擎、故此勝利尤爲可貴云、英皇及皇后首相海外自治部大臣及航空部大臣皆來電致賀、

The Vice-Chairman of the Race Committee, Cole, said that Scott and Black's courage, perseverance, determination, and aviation skills were unprecedented in the history of aviation. The plane they flew was British-made, and the engine that propelled it was also British-made, so this victory is especially valuable. The King and Queen, the Prime Minister, the Secretary of State for Overseas Territories, and the Secretary of State for Aviation all sent telegrams of congratulations.

創飛行新紀錄

Setting a New Flight Record

按史白二人由英抵達爾文港、僅費五十一小時二十六分鐘、較去年澳飛行家烏爾姆六日十七小時四十五分之紀錄、縮少四日强、後因引擎兩具已損其一一、故此後途中僅用引擎一具、彼等在達爾文港勾留最久、但尚不及二小時半、其耐勞精神、於此可見、

According to reports, Scott and Black only spent 51 hours and 26 minutes traveling from England to Darwin, shortening the record of 6 days, 17 hours, and 45 minutes set by Australian aviator Ulm last year by more than four days. Later, because one of the two engines was damaged, they only used one engine for the rest of the trip. They stayed the longest in Darwin, but it was still less than two and a half hours, which shows their endurance.

兩氏之奇績、到處受人讚揚、其體力之强健、實非常人所及、彼等在達爾文港休憇不足兩小時半、此爲自邁爾登都飛行塲出發後最長之休憇、彼等以五十一小時二十六分飛抵達爾文港、較之烏爾姆以六日十七小時四十五分飛畢同一航程而獲之速度紀錄幾快五日、此爲史考特第三次飛行於該航程、一九三二年史氏曾造成英澳間航空速度新紀錄、以八日二十小時四十七分由英倫飛抵達爾文港、然以今之速度與舊日較、則不可同日語矣、（二十三日路透電）

The two men's remarkable achievements have been praised everywhere. Their physical strength is beyond the reach of ordinary people. Their rest in Darwin was less than two and a half hours, which was their longest rest since departing from Mildenhall Aerodrome. They flew to Darwin in 51 hours and 26 minutes, which is almost five days faster than Ulm's speed record of 6 days, 17 hours, and 45 minutes for the same journey. This is Scott's third flight on this route. In 1932, Scott set a new air speed record between England and Australia, flying from London to Darwin in 8 days, 20 hours, and 47 minutes, but today's speed cannot be compared with the past. (Reuters, 23rd)

（倫敦）此次英澳飛行此比賽、錦標爲英國飛行家史考特所得、而其飛行之時間、復超出一切預料之上、按史氏爲一青年駕駛員、年方三十一歲、其父爲一音樂隊領班、有聲於時、幼時在韋斯脫門斯特學校求釜、及十九歲、取得駕駛員資格、不久卽入英國皇家空軍爲飛行員、如是者歷四年之久、嗣在英澳定期航空綫充駕駛員又歷四年、渠曾兩次保持英澳航空速度紀錄、一次在一九三一年以九天四小時造成紀錄、又一次在一九三二年、以八天二十小時又造成新紀錄、以故渠對於英澳間航程極爲熟悉云、史氏同伴勃萊克氏亦爲一熟練之駕駛員、前曾在東菲洲爲飛行家多年、以駕駛術優良、接連獲奬三年云、（二十三日哈瓦斯電）

(London) In this England-Australia flight race, the trophy was won by the British aviator Scott, and his flying time exceeded all expectations. According to reports, Scott is a young pilot, only 31 years old. His father was a band leader, famous at the time. He studied at Westminster School in his youth, and at the age of 19, he obtained a pilot's license. Soon after, he joined the Royal Air Force as a pilot, serving for four years. Later, he served as a pilot on the regular England-Australia airline for another four years. He has held the England-Australia air speed record twice, once in 1931, setting a record of 9 days and 4 hours, and again in 1932, setting a new record of 8 days and 20 hours. Therefore, he is very familiar with the England-Australia route. Scott's companion, Black, is also a skilled pilot, who has been an aviator in East Africa for many years. Due to his excellent piloting skills, he has won awards for three consecutive years. (Havas, 23rd)

抵最後稽核站

Arriving at the Final Checking Station

墨爾缽　英澳間之航空競賽今日第一名可抵目的地、英航空家史考特與白拉克可何奪得錦標、其機中之引擎一具、雖已受損、然今晨七時　（上海時間爲午後二時）稍過當可安降於墨爾缽目的地、果爾、則其平均速度爲每小時逾一百五十哩、兩航空家於昨日午後一時三十分飛離達爾文港、午後十時四十分抵查里鎭、卽最後稽核站、以時間計算共飛程一千三百八十九哩、爲每小時平均飛行一百五十二哩、旣抵查里鎭、卽將所駕之契星號飛機詳騐一過、繼乃裝載僅呈供飛達墨爾缽之燃料、俾速率可以增高、兩航空家在塲監視一切、狀殊不耐、蓋是時分陰亦至足賽貴也、迨諸事完畢、兩人復躍入機中、揮手向塲上歡呼之羣衆告别、軋軋升空、而向其最後目的地猛進、彼等一旦到達、可獲奬金萬鎊及值價五百鎊以上之金杯一事、然物質的榮譽、猶不若精神的榮譽之可貴也、

Melbourne: The first place winner of the England-Australia air race can arrive at the destination today. The English aviators Scott and Black can win the trophy. Although one of the engines in their plane has been damaged, it should be able to safely land at the Melbourne destination shortly after 7:00 this morning (2:00 PM Shanghai time). If so, then their average speed will be over 150 miles per hour. The two aviators flew from Darwin at 1:30 PM yesterday and arrived at Charleville, the final checking station, at 10:40 PM. According to the time, the total flight was 1,389 miles, with an average speed of 152 miles per hour. After arriving at Charleville, they thoroughly checked the de Havilland Comet aircraft they were flying, and then loaded only enough fuel to reach Melbourne, so that the speed could be increased. The two aviators supervised everything on the field, looking very impatient, because every minute and second was precious at that time. When everything was completed, the two men jumped back into the plane, waved goodbye to the cheering crowd on the field, and took off with a creak, heading towards their final destination. Once they arrive, they can win a prize of 10,000 pounds and a gold cup worth over 500 pounds, but the material honor is not as valuable as the spiritual honor.

引擎毁損其一

One Engine Damaged

當達爾文港發出急電、謂史白二氏所駕飛機之引擎一具、已受損不適於用、於是全世界爲之失望、蓋恐修理需時、因而誤事也、但二人在達爾文港停留僅兩小時二十七分、卽復出發、於是衆復大慰、當赴查理之途中、修好之引擎、汽缸復損、故大部分航程僅用引擎一具飛行、旣抵查里鎭、機師復併力修理引擎、當兩航空家飛離該地時、引擎發聲雖佳、而猶覺遲鈍也、墨爾缽民衆聞兩航空家自查里鎭出發消息、卽羣趨跑馬塲以待其至、荷蘭王家航空公司總經理浦萊斯曼已電該公司駐墨爾鉢經理、囑其以大花圈一事贈史考特與白拉克、其上綴有（足下之航空技術與忍耐、不勝欽佩）數言、（廿三日路透電）

When Darwin sent an urgent telegram saying that one of the engines of the plane flown by Scott and Black had been damaged and was unfit for use, the whole world was disappointed, fearing that the repair would take time and thus delay the event. However, the two men stayed in Darwin for only two hours and twenty-seven minutes before setting off again, so everyone was greatly relieved. On the way to Charleville, the repaired engine's cylinder was damaged again, so for most of the journey, they flew with only one engine. After arriving in Charleville, the mechanics worked together to repair the engine. When the two aviators flew away from the location, the engine sounded good, but it still felt sluggish. When the people of Melbourne heard the news that the two aviators had departed from Charleville, they flocked to the racetrack to await their arrival. The General Manager of the Royal Dutch Airlines, Plesman, has wired the company's manager in Melbourne, instructing him to present Scott and Black with a large wreath, with the words "Your aviation skills and endurance are admirable." (Reuters, 23rd)

雙親中心欣慰

Parents Delighted

史考特之父在倫敦語路透訪員、渠子刻已在一萬二千哩之外、此幾爲使人不可輕信之事、恍若往另一世界、但猶在此世界中、渠甚感謝上蒼云、白拉克之母語路透訪員、謂渠子似乘魔毯而行云

Scott's father told a Reuters reporter in London that his son was now 12,000 miles away, which was almost unbelievable, like going to another world, but still in this world. He was very grateful to God. Black's mother told a Reuters reporter that her son seemed to be traveling on a magic carpet.

英雄匹偶佳人

Hero, Partner, and Beauty

（倫敦）　英女伶台斯芒女士今日語路透訪員、謂白拉克飛離邁爾登郝飛行塲前、曾向求婚、渠告以俟奪得競賽錦標後、再予答復、白氏他日回至英倫時、渠或予以答覆、女士又謂史考特與白拉克平安無恙、渠聞之不勝歡忭、渠曾贈白以金火柴匣一、上鐫吉語、白氏出發前曾以渠之肖像三幀置於機室云、此誠航空競賽中之佳話也、（二十三日路透電）

(London) The English actress Miss Theismann told a Reuters reporter today that Black had proposed to her before flying from Mildenhall Aerodrome. She told him that she would give him an answer after winning the race trophy. She might give him an answer when Black returns to England in the future. The lady also said that she was very happy to hear that Scott and Black were safe and sound. She had given Black a gold matchbox with auspicious words engraved on it. Black had placed three portraits of her in the cabin before departure. This is truly a beautiful story in the air race. (Reuters, 23rd)

荷美互爭亞軍

Dutch and American Contest for Second Place

荷飛行家派門蒂曷與摩爾所駕之機陶格拉斯號由達爾文港向查里鎭猛進、而於上午八時四十五分飛抵、越一小時十五分、復登程向墨爾缽進發、該機旋發出乞救電、顯已迷途、翱翔維多利亞邦胡丹迦之天空、按陶格拉斯號由新加坡飛至達爾文港、中途曾停留三次、昨夜十一時抵達爾文港後、停八分鐘卽飛趨查里鎭、航程長一千三百八十九哩、至今晨二時十五分已出現於昆斯蘭之克朗扣里天空、開足速力向前進、

The Dutch aviators Parmentier and Moll, flying the Douglas aircraft, rushed from Darwin to Charleville, arriving at 8:45 AM. After an hour and fifteen minutes, they set off again towards Melbourne. The plane then sent out a distress call, apparently lost, soaring in the skies of Wodonga, Victoria. According to reports, the Douglas aircraft flew from Singapore to Darwin, stopping three times along the way. After arriving in Darwin at 11:00 PM last night, it stopped for eight minutes and then flew to Charleville, a journey of 1,389 miles. At 2:15 AM this morning, it appeared in the skies of Cloncurry, Queensland, moving forward at full speed.

美飛行家唐納與潘邦所駕之機、今晨六時五十分飛抵達爾文港、旋於八時四十八分復升空向查里鎭進發、據唐納語路透訪員、彼等一路平順深以爲慰云、（二十三日路透電）

The American aviators Donner and Pangborn, flying their plane, arrived in Darwin at 6:50 AM this morning, and then took off again towards Charleville at 8:48 AM. According to Donner, speaking to a Reuters reporter, they were very pleased that the journey was smooth. (Reuters, 23rd)

餘機遠落於後

Other Planes Lag Far Behind

至其餘諸機、皆遠落於後、英飛行家瓊司與華勒昨離阿拉哈巴後、旋因引擎有損、復折回修理、嗣於二時四十三分飛抵新加坡、此爲過第三稽核站之第四機、彼等平均速度每小時達一百十三分抵巴達維亞、復因引擎遥有損、覊留該處、墨克里哥與華克之機旣抵阿拉哈巴、稍停卽飛往喀爾喀特、而於午後六時四十一分到達、賴愛特之機今晨七時二十八分飛抵報達米爾羅斯之機午後十二時零五分亦抵報達、希威特與凱氏之機今晨四時零五分飛抵迦拉基、越兩小時續登丹麥飛行家漢生之機昨晨九時四十四分飛抵報達、旋卽續發、而於午後二時十九分抵布夏、繼進抵迦拉基、但延至午夜始赴阿拉哈巴、萊煦之機昨夜十一時離報達、旋於迦拉基發見油池滲漏、大約須明晨始能續發、（廿三日路透電）

As for the other planes, they are far behind. The English aviators Jones and Waller, after leaving Allahabad yesterday, turned back for repairs due to engine damage, and then flew to Singapore at 2:43 PM. This is the fourth plane to pass the third checking station. Their average speed reached 113 per hour to Batavia. The engine was damaged again, so they were detained there. McGregor and Walker's plane arrived in Allahabad, and after a short stop, flew to Calcutta, arriving at 6:41 PM. Wright's plane arrived in Baghdad at 7:28 AM this morning. Mirros' plane also arrived in Baghdad at 12:05 PM this afternoon. Hewitt and Kay's plane arrived in Karachi at 4:05 AM this morning, and continued two hours later. The Danish aviator Hansen's plane arrived in Baghdad at 9:44 AM yesterday morning, and then continued, arriving in Bushire at 2:19 PM, and then advanced to Karachi, but it was delayed until midnight before going to Allahabad. Lash's plane left Baghdad at 11:00 PM last night, and then found an oil leak in Karachi, and it will probably not be able to continue until tomorrow morning. (Reuters, 23rd)

荷飛機兼程而進

Dutch Plane Advances at Full Speed

蘭荷蘭航空家派門蒂曷與摩爾所駕之陶格拉斯號飛機、現方由達爾文港向查里鎭進發、該飛機由新加坡飛往達爾文港、途中曾停頓三次、第一次乃在巴達維亞、第二次乃在藍浦班島、（東羣島之一）、昨日午後三時五十七分飛離該島、後又降於哥帮嗣於昨夜七時五十分由該處飛往達爾文港、而於十一時到達、停留僅八分鐘、卽飛往一千三百八十九哩外之查里鎭、

The Dutch aviators Parmentier and Moll's Douglas aircraft are now heading from Darwin to Charleville. The aircraft stopped three times on the way from Singapore to Darwin. The first time was in Batavia, the second time was on Rambang Island (one of the eastern islands). Yesterday afternoon at 3:57 PM, they flew from the island, and later landed in Kupang, and then flew from there to Darwin at 7:50 PM last night, arriving at 11:00 PM. After stopping for only eight minutes, they flew to Charleville, 1,389 miles away.

美飛機追逐在後

American Plane Chases Behind

又美國航空家唐納大佐與潘邦則方由新加坡直趨達爾文港、至其餘諸機、則皆瞠乎其後矣、

Also, the American aviators Colonel Donner and Pangborn are heading straight from Singapore to Darwin. As for the other planes, they are all far behind.

美國航空家唐納與潘邦曾奮勇追逐荷機陶格拉斯號而未成功、彼等於昨日午後三時二十七分飛離新加坡、約後荷機八小時彼等出發時、擬一氣飛達達爾文港、中途不作停留（二十三日路透電）

The American aviators Donner and Pangborn bravely chased the Dutch plane Douglas but failed. They flew from Singapore at 3:27 PM yesterday, about eight hours after the Dutch plane departed. When they departed, they planned to fly to Darwin in one go without stopping. (Reuters, 23rd)

與賽僅剩十四架

Only Fourteen Planes Remain in the Race

原來從邁爾登郝出發者共二十機、今吉爾曼因機墮殞命、而莫理遜夫婦等五機又因機損退出、故現仍參加航空競賽者殆僅有十四機、其中除三機已飛過新加坡外、餘者猶沉滯途中、（二十三日路透社電）

Originally, there were twenty planes that departed from Mildenhall. Now, Gilman died due to a plane crash, and five planes, including the Morrisons, withdrew due to plane damage. Therefore, there are probably only fourteen planes still participating in the air race. Among them, except for three planes that have flown past Singapore, the rest are still delayed along the way. (Reuters, 23rd)

英軍官不幸殉身

British Officer Dies Tragically

最不幸者、爲英航空軍官吉爾曼與其同伴裴恩士所駕之機、昨日在意境墜地着火、二人同遭焚斃、其機參加速度與障碍競賽、自始卽遭遇逆境、彼等爲星期六日競賽開始前最後飛抵邁爾登郝飛行塲者、出發未久、因引擎有損、降落里昻附近之阿伏爾、當彼等在瑪特拉附近飛過亞平寗山脈時、因速度太高、機翻墜地、頓時起火、據路透社探悉、其機已爲七八年之舊物、斐萊航空公司對於該機之狀况不負責任、謂該機顯以舊貨購諸航空部者、

The most unfortunate thing is that the plane driven by the British Air Force officer Gilman and his companion Baynes crashed and caught fire in Italy yesterday, and the two were burned to death. Their plane participated in the speed and obstacle race, and encountered adversity from the beginning. They were the last to fly to Mildenhall Aerodrome before the race started on Saturday. Not long after departure, due to engine damage, they landed in Avord near Lyon. When they flew over the Apennine Mountains near Mattela, due to excessive speed, the plane overturned and crashed, and immediately caught fire. According to Reuters, their plane was seven or eight years old. Fairey Aviation Company is not responsible for the condition of the plane, saying that the plane was apparently purchased from the Aviation Department as old goods.

轟炸機毁人無恙

Bomber Destroyed, But People Safe

新加坡　英國皇家航空車之轟炸機一架、昨晨因英澳間航空競賽事由阿洛爾斯太飛出、嗣杳無消息、今已經覓見毁於卓賀爾之庫蘭附近森林中、機中之人均無恙、無一受傷者、但機已全毁、（二十三日路透電）

Singapore: A bomber of the British Royal Air Force flew out of Alor Setar yesterday morning due to the England-Australia air race, but there was no news afterwards. Now it has been found destroyed in the forest near Kulai, Johor. The people in the plane are all safe and sound, with no one injured, but the plane has been completely destroyed. (Reuters, 23rd)

比敎授上升同温層

Professor Piccard Ascends into the Stratosphere

續作科學探險

Continuing Scientific Exploration

美國密起根地朋比敎授畢卡德夫婦今日乘其巨大氣球上升同温層作科學探騐、觀此名科學家偕其地人升空者祗寥寥數人、此次升空宗旨不在造成新紀錄、在搜集科學材料蓋以試騐宇宙光他日可以應用也、畢敎授之弟亦爲有名之科學家現在瑞士籌備、擬自阿爾帕斯山升同温層探騐、（廿二日國民電）

Professor Piccard and his wife of Michigan, USA, ascended into the stratosphere in their giant balloon today for scientific exploration. Few of these famous scientists ascend into the sky with locals. The purpose of this ascent is not to create a new record, but to collect scientific materials to test the cosmic rays that can be used in the future. Professor Piccard's brother is also a famous scientist and is now preparing in Switzerland to ascend into the stratosphere from the Alps for exploration. (National News, 22nd)

Leader of the All-India Congress

Bombay Gandhi announced today that he had decided to resign from the leadership of the All-India Congress and will no longer be an ordinary member. It is heard that he intends to devote all his energy to rectifying rural industries in the future. (Reuters, 23rd)

國際紅會席上

At the International Red Cross Meeting

俄提弭戰議案

Russia Proposes a Motion to End War

付委員會審查

Referred to Committee for Review

（東京）國際紅十字會議、復於二十三日午前九時半起在日本紅十字本會開會、經總會之决定、分爲四大委員會、各部分别担任問題行使討論、以便採决、昨於二十二日由蘇聯代表拉哥布斯基氏所提防止戰爭决議案、已由第一委員會、（法律問題）附議、但現又由該會交與第二委員會（普通問題）、將蘇聨代表之提案予以討論、簽以紅十字聯盟原應從消極之保護事業、更進一步設法防止戰爭、使國際上之糾紛在和平上謀解决策、並宜由各國政府及其國民努力團結一致、對於此事當希望予以决議、聞由該第二委員會卽須向總會提出報告云、（二十三日日聯電）

(Tokyo) The International Red Cross Conference convened again at the Japanese Red Cross headquarters on the 23rd at 9:30 AM. According to the decision of the General Assembly, it was divided into four major committees, each responsible for discussing issues in order to make decisions. The resolution to prevent war proposed by the Soviet representative Lagobsky on the 22nd has been seconded by the First Committee (Legal Issues), but now it has been handed over to the Second Committee (General Issues) by the association to discuss the Soviet representative's proposal, with the signature that the Red Cross League should advance from passive protection efforts to further prevent war, seek solutions to international disputes peacefully, and it is appropriate for governments and their citizens to work together in unity. It is hoped that a resolution will be made on this matter. It is heard that the Second Committee must submit a report to the General Assembly. (Japanese United Press, 23rd)

德敎練艦赴美

German Training Ship Goes to America

啟爾

敎練巡艦卡爾魯號今日載海軍練習生六百人自啟爾出發、作八個月之海上操練、送行者數千人、學生家屬均得上艦握别、該艦啟椗前接德國元首希特勒來電云、（余希望出國之青年至他國時務須保持國家之尊嚴）云、該艦將首往中美、繼至南美、敎練官爲柳特金斯艦長、柳氏語記者云、此行任務在遍訪百年以來僑居南美之德人、使彼等獲新德國之慰智云、十一月十日將有練習艦愛姆頓號往遊印度云、（二十二日國民電）

The Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company Liaises with the Longhai Railway: To Open New Shipping Routes to Tianjin, Guangdong, and Qingdao; The Entire Longhai Line Expected to Be Open to Traffic by Year's End. Since the state-run Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company and the Longhai Railway began their joint transportation operations, business has been very prosperous. Now that the Lianyungang pier has been completed, ships can reliably dock there starting this month. To further expand business, both parties plan to open new shipping routes to ports such as Tianjin, Guangdong, and Qingdao, which will soon be implemented. In addition, Chen Yongjie, head of the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company's Haizhou branch, recently came to Shanghai to report on the current situation in Lianyungang. Huang Zhaotong, director of the Longhai Railway's Transportation Department, also came to Shanghai to discuss important matters. The details of these events are recorded below.

Initial Construction of Lianyungang Completed: The Lianyungang pier, a deep-water port for the Longhai Railway, has been under construction for a long time. The initial phase of construction has now been completed, and ships began docking there on the first of this month. However, only one ship can be accommodated at a time. Construction is still ongoing, and it is expected that three ocean-going vessels can be docked by the end of this year. After the entire project is completed, five vessels can be accommodated. To gain a clear understanding of the port's situation, the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company specifically telegraphed Chen Yongjie, head of its Haizhou branch, to come to Shanghai and report.

Planning Three Joint Transportation Routes: Currently, the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company and the Longhai Railway, in order to expand their business, will open three joint transportation routes: (1) Lianyungang directly to Tianjin, with a stop in Shanghai; (2) Lianyungang directly to Guangzhou, with a stop in Shanghai; (3) Lianyungang directly to Qingdao. The planning for the above-mentioned Tianjin and Guangdong routes has been underway for a long time, and the freight rates and other major aspects have been largely agreed upon. Huang Zhaotong, director of the Longhai Railway's Transportation Department, also came to Shanghai to discuss these matters in person. An agreement will be signed in the coming days, and implementation will begin soon. As for the Qingdao route, it is still in the planning stages.

Entire Longhai Line to Open to Traffic by Year's End: According to information obtained by reporters from the Longhai Railway's Shanghai Joint Transportation Office, the railway has also implemented joint water-land transportation after the opening of the Tongguan to Weinan section. Goods shipped from Shanghai can be directly picked up at Weinan Station. The distance is 74 kilometers, with six stations in between: Dongquan Dian, Huayin, Xiaying, Liuzhi, Huazhou, and Chishui. To the west of Weinan, there are still 58 kilometers, passing through Lingkou, Xinfengzhen, Lintong, Yaocun, Baqiao, and finally to Sian. Currently, track laying and station building are being rushed, and it is expected to be completed by the end of the year. The entire line will be open to traffic on New Year's Day next year.

Chen Yongjie Optimistic About the Future: Since the opening of Lianyungang, the old Yao pier has achieved some success, making the transport of goods from the Northwest to Shanghai particularly convenient. Chen Yongjie, director of the Haizhou branch of the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company, came to Shanghai on official business this time and provided detailed information about the development of joint transportation. The following is a record of his remarks: This year's cotton harvest in Shaanxi is very good, better than in previous years. After being baled in Zhengzhou, it is transported by the Longhai Railway to the old Yao pier, and then loaded onto the company's joint transportation ships to Shanghai. Grains such as raw peanuts, soybeans, and wheat are also extremely congested, mostly shipped from the old Yao pier, no longer transported to Dabu. Therefore, only one ship is currently left running between Shanghai and Dabu. The newly built permanent pier at the old Yao pier docked its maiden voyage ship on Double Tenth Day this year. By January 1st next year, one phase of construction will be completed, allowing for the docking of one more vessel. By April, the entire project will be completed, allowing for the berthing of three ships simultaneously. The pier is 32 feet deep at high tide and 23 feet deep at low tide. The amount of Northwest goods transported from the old Yao pier to Shanghai each month has reached 20,000 tons, and the amount transported from Shanghai to the old Yao pier is 5,000 tons per month. The company originally dispatched three ships to operate, but now, due to the completion of the pier and the congestion of incoming goods, it feels insufficient. Therefore, starting next month, it has been decided to add another ship, using four ships for transport. The opening of the Lianyungang old Yao pier and the unloading of ships at the newly built (permanent) pier is about half completed in terms of the entire project. The urgent task at hand is the construction of land-based buildings, building a six-story building to house the offices of the Longhai Railway Bureau, the Shanghai Merchant Steam Navigation Company's Joint Transportation Haizhou Branch, the Lianyungang Port Authority, and the Customs Office. In addition, a breakwater will be built using stones from Lianyungang Mountain, filling them into the sea. Extremely large machinery will be used to dredge the mud from the sea mouth and inside and outside the port, so that 10,000-ton giant ships can travel without obstruction, etc.

Fei Dasheng Discusses the Yuqi Silk Factory's Improved Silk Quality: The silk produced is highly praised overseas; Hoping that silk merchants across the country will thoroughly awaken. 14

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, China's silk industry has been declining year by year. On the one hand, it is due to the dumping of Japanese silk, which has seized China's foreign markets. On the other hand, the lack of improvement in silk production and the poor quality of silk are also major reasons. Recently, leaders in the silk industry in Jiangsu Province, in view of this situation, initiated the establishment of the Yuqi Silk Factory, using the latest scientific methods to reel raw silk on behalf of manufacturers. The silk produced has already won international recognition. Fei Dasheng, the manager of the factory, came to Shanghai yesterday to meet with Zeng Yangfu, the director of the Zhejiang Construction Department, to discuss the silk industry. Yesterday, a reporter from the Shen Shi News Agency specially interviewed Fei at his lodging, and he provided the following information.

Improved Silk Quality Gains Fame Abroad: According to Fei, the poor sales of Chinese silk in recent years are due to the fact that Chinese silk merchants have paid too little attention to improving the quality of silk, resulting in almost the entire foreign market being occupied by Japanese silk. Now, Wuxi silk merchants feel that in order to save the silk industry, it is necessary to thoroughly improve silk production. They specifically commissioned the silk production department of the Hushu Pass Provincial Women's Sericulture School to handle it. After a year of trial operation, the results were remarkable. The raw silk produced was shipped to the United Kingdom and the United States and was praised as the best silk in China. Therefore, in June of this year, the Wuxi Yuqi Ruilun Silk Factory was renovated with multiple silk reeling machines and other equipment were added, and the factory was operated and reformed according to the school's approach. Labor recruitment and training began at the beginning of last month, and the factory was named the Yuqi Silk Factory. It is now in operation.

Unlike the Exploitation of Capitalists: Fei continued, The organization of silk factories has always been that raw materials, silk production, and sales are all in the hands of capitalists. However, the Yuqi Silk Factory is an independent entity, and sales and raw materials are not related. The operation of the silk factory is divided into three parts, so that each can focus its energy on research. The Yuqi Silk Factory has two major characteristics: (1) Implementing rural relief, making every effort to reduce costs, and making industry a sideline of agriculture. The factory is located in a rural area, employing farmers from nearby areas as female workers, so as to make farmers' economies prosperous and their lives stable. (2) The factory implements factory schooling, seeking the happiness of the majority of workers, and is absolutely not like the exploitation of workers by capitalists. Therefore, workers have good cultivation, and the quality of the silk produced must be excellent, so as to promote sales overseas and be able to regain the market that has been seized from us.

Hoping that Silk Merchants Across the Country Will Awaken: Fei concluded, Saving the decline of Chinese raw silk cannot be achieved by empty talk. It cannot be solved by simply promoting sales and neglecting the fundamentals. Silk producers must work hard to improve the quality of silk, and cooperate with sales manufacturers to divide labor. The Yuqi Silk Factory is organized based on this principle. At the beginning of September, 200 workers were recruited and divided into five batches to enter the factory for training. More than half of those who can reel at a high level of 90 points or more. Whether it will be possible to save our endangered silk industry in the future remains to be seen through the efforts of colleagues and the awakening of silk manufacturers across the country.

Four Requests from Stamp Tax Branch Bureaus: The Provincial Bureau Believes the Reasons Are Sufficient; Permission Granted to Forward to the Ministry of Finance. The various branch bureaus of stamp tax in Jiangsu Province, due to the significant losses suffered by the Ministry's order to abolish and replace stamp tax tickets, have organized a joint office at No. 61, Lane 576, Yuyuan Road, Shanghai, to petition the Provincial Bureau, requesting permission to return the stored stamps, reissue funds, and issue severance pay. In addition, they request that the Review Committee for Cases Violating the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax be extended to complete its work, so as to pursue the fines payable by those who have been fined, and to facilitate the conclusion of other matters. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, representatives of the heads of various district branch bureaus went to the Provincial Bureau on Avenue Edward VII to petition. After Director Sheng met them, the representatives stated the difficulties of each bureau and the reasons for the four requests. The Provincial Bureau also recognized that the losses suffered by the branch bureaus were indeed factual and that the reasons for the requests were sufficient. However, due to the Ministry's orders, this was the case nationwide, not just in one province, so it was not convenient to make a decision on its own. Permission was granted to forward the request to the Ministry and to plead reasonably. The representatives were satisfied with the Provincial Bureau's expression of sincerity and then took their leave, waiting for relief. If a satisfactory conclusion is not reached, the bureaus will jointly delay the handover and conduct further expanded joint petitions.

Trade Bureau: Introducing and Promoting Graphite and Bean Cake Powder; Spain Needs 100 Tons of Bean Cake Powder; Manufacturers Can Contact the Bureau Directly. Yesterday, the Guidance Division of the International Trade Bureau announced that graphite, also known as pencil lead, is a type of carbonaceous mineral that cannot be eroded by acids. Therefore, it is an indispensable raw material in the metallurgical industry. It also has a wide range of other uses, such as in the manufacture of crucibles, pencils, batteries, paints, stove powder, lubricants, etc. Currently, Yihuang County, Jiangxi Province, produces a large amount of graphite with a high carbon content. Manufacturers who need it can contact the bureau, and samples are available. Bean cake powder is the residue from making bean cakes and can be used as feed and fertilizer. It can also be used to make glue in the chemical industry. Currently, the Spanish company "Marrakech" needs 100 tons of bean cake powder. Manufacturers who wish to promote sales abroad should send a letter to the bureau for introduction.

Charitable Organizations: Jointly Organize Disaster Relief for Haiyan; Representatives from the Jisheng Society and the China International Famine Relief Commission Have Departed; County Magistrate Jiang Huihong Returns to the County After Completing Discussions in Shanghai. Yu Zuoting: The Course of Mediating the Elephant Shell Dispute; The Pharmaceutical Industry Has Accepted the Proposed Conditions. The elephant shell dispute between the Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Association and the Ningxian Dongjiang Fritillaria Sales Cooperative has not yet been resolved. The day before yesterday at noon, Yu Zuoting, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, specially hosted a banquet for representatives of both parties at the Shipping Club on Guangdong Road to formally mediate the dispute. Those present included Cen Ziliang, a representative of the national pharmaceutical industry, Zhou Weixing, a representative of the cooperative (represented by Tang from the Bank of Communications), Weng Yangqing, a representative of the Ningbo Four Pharmaceutical Firms, Wang Yingbin, secretary of the Zhejiang Construction Department who served as mediator, and Yu Zuoting, a total of five people. During the meeting, Yu first spoke, generally hoping that both parties would pay attention to reality and not simply make lofty statements, so as to avoid getting farther and farther away from the path to resolving the case. He also hoped that the representatives of both parties would sincerely exchange views, conduct detailed research separately, and then he would convene both parties to sign a contract and formally mediate. The representatives of both parties then exchanged views, and the meeting adjourned at about 3:00 PM. The National Pharmaceutical Industry Association specially convened an executive committee meeting at its office on Ningbo Road at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday to report the details of Yu's mediation. After a detailed discussion, the meeting adjourned at 6:20 PM. According to Chairman Cen Ziliang after the meeting, the meeting decided to accept Yu's enthusiasm and formally put forward specific conditions to the cooperative. The content of the conditions still needs to be carefully discussed and cannot be disclosed.

Outline of the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee: A Special Dispatch from the National News Agency in Nanjing states that the organizational outline of the newly established Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee is as follows: Article 1: This committee is jointly organized by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, entrusted by the Ministry of Finance. Article 2: This committee shall have three members, one each appointed by the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. One of the three members shall be mutually elected as chairman and reported to the Ministry of Finance for record. Article 3: The standard for the daily collection of the equalization tax shall be determined by the committee. Article 4: In order to meet the needs of the market, the committee may entrust the Central Bank to buy and sell foreign exchange and bullion to stabilize the market. Article 5: When necessary, the committee may entrust the Central Bank to export and import gold and silver. Article 6: The government's equalization tax on silver shall be allocated to the committee as a market stabilization fund and ordered by the Ministry of Finance to be delivered to the Central Bank for separate storage. Article 7: If there is a loss in stabilizing the exchange market by the committee, the funds in the preceding article shall be used first. If there is still a shortfall, it shall be borne by the Ministry of Finance. Article 8: All committee proceedings and accounts shall be reported to the Ministry of Finance on a monthly basis for record. Article 9: The committee may selectively transfer personnel from the three banks to assist in handling affairs. Article 10: This outline shall be implemented upon approval by the Ministry of Finance.

Hu Translates "On Japanese Zaibatsu" to Be Published: The contents of the Japanese zaibatsu are not only lacking a systematic cost in our country, but even in Japan to this day, there is no detailed record. The author of this book, Suzuki Mosaburo, understands the situation of the zaibatsu and has conducted painstaking investigations. He writes frankly and analyzes and criticizes all the large, medium, and small zaibatsu and local zaibatsu in Japan one by one. The book was published at the end of last month. Mr. Hu Chunyun, in view of the detailed content of the book, has begun to translate it, and it is expected to be completed next month. The content is divided into general theory and specific theory. In addition to the three Mitsui, Mitsubishi, and Sumitomo zaibatsu, the book also lists the emerging capitalist zaibatsu institutions in Japan, the activity centers of the zaibatsu in industry, and the monopoly of the zaibatsu capital, which are complete and exhaustive. It is the only data for studying Japanese politics, economy, and finance. The entire book consists of 80,000 to 90,000 words, translated and annotated in simple classical Chinese. It is thought to be eagerly anticipated by those concerned about Japanese finance.

He was honest and diligent, and was respected by all his colleagues. Last week, he contracted a minor illness, but he still insisted on working. After returning home to rest, he was expected to recover soon, but unfortunately, he passed away at 10:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 22nd) due to a sudden change in his condition. We are deeply saddened. Mr. Hu was 62 years old. The coffin will be encoffined at the Shanghai Funeral Home this afternoon. The simple hearse and white horse add to the sadness.

Female Officer Wei Jiechen: Attacked and Killed with 22 Knife Wounds in Broad Daylight; Two Thugs Leapt Out of the Deep Forest: Left Shoulder, Side, Back, Waist, Chest, Neck, Head. At 10:40 AM yesterday (the 23rd), Wei Jiechen, a first-class patrol officer from the Zhoujiaqiao Police Station of the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau in western Shanghai, was riding in a rickshaw when he was suddenly attacked by two thugs wielding sharp blades near the west side of the back gate of Zhaofeng Garden on Jessfield Road. He was stabbed more than 22 times and seriously injured. The detailed account of the incident is recorded below.

More Than Twenty Years of Devotion to Duty: Wei Jiechen, courtesy name Jingxian, 39 years old, from Xian County, Hebei Province, is a first-class patrol officer stationed at the Zhoujiaqiao Police Station of the Caojiadu Bureau in western Shanghai. His home is near the station. He has an elderly mother and a wife of similar age. He has no children. In 1912, he worked in Tianjin with Xu Guoliang, the former police chief. In 1913, he came to Shanghai with Xu and served as the head of the patrol team. Later, he was promoted to patrol officer and transferred to the Second District. In June 1929, he was transferred to the Zhoujiaqiao Police Station and has been there for more than twenty years, devoted to his duty. He has always been valued by the various district chiefs. He is also quite harmonious with the local gentry and merchants and has always been peaceful in his dealings with others.

Attacked on the Way Back to the Station by Rickshaw: Director Wang Dasui convened a meeting at the bureau at 9:00 AM yesterday morning to jointly discuss all aspects of duty. Wei attended the meeting. After the meeting ended at 10:00 AM, he chatted with the other patrol officers for about half an hour and then hired a rickshaw to return to the station. When he arrived at the side of utility pole No. 129 on the west side of the back gate of Zhaofeng Garden on Jessfield Road (the south side of the road is Zhaofeng Garden, and the north side of the road is St. John's Garden, a place with few pedestrians in the middle of a deep forest), two thugs suddenly came from behind. They were both wearing blue cloth shirts and pants. One jumped forward.

Stabbed 22 Times All Over His Body: One of the thugs rushed forward first, grabbed the rickshaw hood with his left hand, and stabbed Wei in the back of the neck with a sharp blade in his right hand. Wei felt pain but thought it was a familiar person teasing him. He looked back and realized that things were not good. He jumped out of the rickshaw. The two thugs each held up their sharp blades and stabbed Wei frantically. The rickshaw puller shouted for help. Wei fainted and fell to the ground. The two thugs, seeing that their goal had been achieved, abandoned their murder weapons on the ground in the garden and fled. At that time, Zhou Fushan, a gardener, and Wang Agui, who was selling peanuts on the road nearby, heard the alarm and rushed to take a look. They immediately reported to Teng Guanghui, a guard at Post No. 2 (although it was about 500 steps away). At the same time, N. P. Baienoff, an Englishman in Zhaofeng Garden, happened to be passing by in car No. 3800. He saw it and immediately instructed the driver to help Wei into the car and send him to the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road for treatment. He suffered two wounds to his left shoulder, three to his left side, three to his back, one to his left and right waist, six to his chest, two to his neck, one to his left waist, and three to his head, a total of 22 wounds. Blood was everywhere on the ground.

All Police Officers Mobilized to Pursue the Suspects: Director Wang received the report and immediately led Patrol Officers Long and Yang and the entire team of sergeants and detectives, including Squad Leader Wu Kezhong and Cao Chuqiao, and all the detectives to the scene of the incident to apprehend the suspects. They searched without success. After a detailed investigation, he immediately reported to the director and ordered his subordinates to arrest the suspects as soon as possible. At the same time, the Jing'an Temple Police Station received the report and dispatched detectives led by the Western Detective to rush to pursue the suspects without success. They found two triangular, newly sharpened murder weapons (about eight inches long) on the grass in the garden and immediately sent them to the bureau. Director Wang then took the patrol officers to the hospital to visit Wei. Wei was still able to speak with difficulty. According to the doctor, his lungs have been damaged because he has just been given a blood transfusion. The wounds are about two inches deep and he is still in danger. His life is still uncertain. The reason for the stabbing is still unclear. Three blood-stained shirts have also been brought back to the bureau. Director Wang then sent police officers to question Zhou Fushan, the gardener, Wang Agui, who sold peanuts, and Wei Huashan, the rickshaw puller. They were temporarily released on bail.

Years ago, Shen Songshi, due to difficult living conditions, contracted Wanhua to be a singer in a brothel. At that time, the younger daughter, Fudi, would go to the brothel from time to time to visit her sister. It happened that Zhang Tinggui, a local man who was a compradore at the New Feng Foreign Firm at No. 117 Sassoon House on the Bund in Nanjing Road, who was 38 years old, would often go to Wanhua's brothel to sing and drink. Therefore, he met Fudi. At first sight, he was captivated by her. Later, he even rented a room in a hotel and consummated their relationship. After several rendezvous, Fudi became pregnant. Her mother found out, but since the deed was done, she tolerated it. Unexpectedly, Zhang stopped visiting and treated her like a stranger. Shen Songshi had no choice but to sue Zhang in the First Special Court as a guardian on behalf of Fudi, accusing him of rape of a minor under the age of 16 and harming public morals. The initial trial was lost. Shen Songshi was not satisfied and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. The High Court approved the appeal and conducted the trial on the 17th of this month. At that time, the appellant stated that Fudi had just given birth to a daughter on the 11th of this month, so she did not appear in court. Only the lawyer Yang Qianmao appeared in court and stated everything. At that time, the interrogator stated that the key to the case was whether Fudi was under the age of 16, so he declared the debate between the two parties in court over and announced the conclusion. The judgment was scheduled to be announced on the 23rd of this month. As reported in this newspaper, neither party appeared in court yesterday, the day of the scheduled judgment. Judge Yu took the seat in Criminal Court 1 and read the main text of the judgment, stating that the appeal was dismissed. However, it is said that the appellant is still not satisfied and will appeal to the Supreme Court again.

Sports News, 1934-1935: Important Contents of New Basketball Rules

Many Changes to Old Rules

This Year's West Qing (Games) Will Adopt New Rules

The Basketball Rules Committee of the United States has announced the 1934-1935 basketball rules, which include several changes to the old rules. The West Qing Basketball Championship this year will be held according to the new rules. The important contents of the new rules are translated as follows:

(1) Article 1, Section 1 stipulates that the minimum area for a newly built basketball court shall be 74 feet long and 42 feet wide.

(2) Article 3, Section 1: The basketball net, which used to wrap around the hoop, is now attached below the hoop.

(3) Article 4, Section 1 stipulates that the circumference of the ball shall not be less than 29 and a half inches, and shall not be greater than 30 and a half inches.

(4) Article 5, Section 2: Two minutes before the game, each team must report the names, numbers, and positions of the players to the recorder, otherwise they will be penalized with a technical foul. The purpose of this article is to ensure that the game starts on time and avoid unnecessary delays. At the same time, Article 3, Section 2 stipulates that if a team delays the start of each half after the referee blows the whistle, it will be penalized with a technical foul for every minute of delay.

(5) Article 5, Section 6: The minimum height of the jersey number of the player is 4 inches.

(6) Article 6, Sections 1 and 2 stipulate the adoption of a dual-referee system.

(7) Article 9, Section 3: Regarding middle school games, it is decided to adopt the (sudden death) method. If the scores of the two teams are still equal in the second overtime period, the team that scores first in the second overtime period shall be determined as the winner. This method can also be used in the first overtime period for other games. This method avoids excessive fatigue after prolonged overtime.

(8) Article 10, Section 1: Any ball that goes out of bounds must be handed over to the player throwing the ball by the referee. At the same time, Article 14, Section 10 stipulates that if a player violates this rule, the ball must be immediately handed over to the nearest referee.

(9) Article 11, Section 1: For game timing, all fouls, whether technical fouls, double fouls, or personal fouls after a successful shot, the time must be paused and not counted. The timing will resume after the jump ball in the center circle. If a free throw after a personal foul is unsuccessful, the time will continue to be calculated after the miss.

(10) Article 15 is divided into three sections, A, B, and C. Section B stipulates that the referee must be forced to punish instructors and coaches who give improper guidance from the sidelines during the game.

Municipal Education Bureau Announces 20

Rules for Middle School Joint Sports Meet

Seven Field Events and Eight Track Events for Men

Four Field Events and Four Track Events for Women

The third Municipal Middle School Joint Sports Meet will be held at Jiaotong University for three days starting on November 8th. Details have been published in various newspapers. The rules of the sports meet have been announced by the Municipal Education Bureau. They are recorded as follows: Article 1: This meeting is sponsored by the Municipal Education Bureau, with the aim of promoting the physical education of middle schools in the city. Article 2: All municipal, registered, and approved private middle schools in the city must have students participating as athletes in this meeting. However, other public middle schools in the city may also select students to apply to participate as athletes in this meeting. Article 3: The venue of this meeting is the playground of the National Jiaotong University on Xujiahui Road. Article 4: The opening date of this meeting is from November 8th to 10th, 23rd year. If necessary, the president of this meeting may decide to change it. Article 5: The mayor serves as the president of this meeting, and the director of the Education Bureau serves as the vice president. Article 6: This meeting has one director of general affairs, who presides over all general affairs, and is divided into two departments: administrative and competitive. Each department has one chief director. The administrative department is divided into six sections: general affairs, accounting, documents, editing, reception, and discipline. The competitive department is divided into two sections: competition and venue. All staff members are hired by the director of the Education Bureau. Article 7: The sports are divided into two categories: group exercises and track and field. The items are as follows: (A) Group Exercise Department: (1) General Assembly Exercise: Each school should send one-tenth of the total number of students to participate as representatives. (2) Group exercises, such as national martial arts, walking, flexibility exercises, gymnastics, and fitness dances. (B) Track and Field Department: (1) Men's Field Events: high jump, long jump, pole vault, triple jump, discus throw, javelin throw, shot put, track events, 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1,500 meters, 110-meter hurdles, 800-meter relay, 1,600-meter relay. (2) Women's Field Events: high jump, long jump, javelin throw, shot put, track events, 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, 400-meter relay. Article 8: For track and field athletes, each person can register for a maximum of three events for men and two events for women, excluding relays. Each school can register a maximum of three people for each department and each event.

(5) Referees: In addition to the championship matches being refereed by the referee committee, ordinary matches will be refereed by the two competing teams in rotation. (6) The meeting adjourned.

Recent News on Polish Culture 27

The Sino-Polish Cultural Association recently translated and described the news about the Polish cultural circle, which is recorded below: (1) Professor Tiechinski, the authority on Polish Latin and Greek cultural history, has won honorary doctorates and honorary professorships from various universities in Europe, and has recently been elected as a member of the Seville World Cultural Association by Spanish scientists. (2) The Polish Academy of Sciences and the University of Vilnius jointly invited Professor Vidolani, a famous Polish scientist, to Turkey to complete his research on cattle breeding that began several years ago. (3) The World Tuberculosis Association recently held a meeting in Warsaw, the capital of Poland, with members, doctors, and scientists from 35 countries attending as representatives. The largest number of representatives came from Italy, France, and Germany. Our country was represented by the ambassador to Poland. (4) The World Women's Sports Competition was held in Brussels, Belgium. The championship was won by the United Kingdom, and Poland was the runner-up. Several records were broken by Polish female athletes. (5) The World Women's Archery Competition was recently held in Sweden. The individual championship was won by Mrs. Siqiejialovah, a Polish female athlete, and the team championship was also won by the Polish team. (6) In the Davis Cup tennis competition, Poland defeated Belgium 4-1 and Estonia and Greece 5-0, so Poland will be able to join the semi-finals in the next competition.

Anhui Local Education Expenses Austerity Measures 28

The Anhui Education Department previously issued points to note when compiling the education budget for each county in the 23rd year of the local government. It stated that before the education budget for the 23rd year is approved, expenditures will be temporarily made according to the original budget for the 22nd year. Later, due to reports of drought in various counties, the Education Department issued measures to maintain local education funds in disaster-stricken counties, ordering each county to refer to the various regulations and consider reducing expenditures. Currently, the reports on the budget from each county are still not complete, and the 23rd year has already begun. The Education Department has issued another notice to each county: 1. Each disaster-stricken county must uniformly spend according to the reduced budget in order to achieve a balance between income and expenditure. 2. If expenditures have already been made according to the budget for the 22nd year, the excess amount should be deducted in installments on a monthly basis and completed within the first half of the year. 3. Counties that have not submitted the budget should uniformly submit it. 4. Each county should submit a monthly statement of income and expenditure in the future.

National Military Training Association 30

Examines the Military Training Results of Various Schools

And Sends Personnel to Talk with the Principals of Various Schools

Military Instructors Should Reside in the School

Since Mr. Jiao Jihua took office as the director of the Municipal National Military Training Committee, he has spared no effort to promote national military education in the city. The number of schools implementing military training this semester has reached more than 70, an increase of half compared with the previous semester. According to Director Jiao yesterday, the recent work of the association is as follows:

Examination Results: The association believes that the military instructors bear heavy responsibilities, and some school authorities do not consult on this matter, resulting in a small number of instructors forming a special position and being negligent in their duties. Therefore, personnel have been sent to various schools in recent days to examine the military instructors' classes and exercises, starting from the China Vocational School.

Contacting Principals: Some schools do not fully understand the situation of military training and are inevitably separated from the military instructors, which greatly affects the future of military training in the school. Therefore, in addition to preparing to invite the Municipal Education Bureau to convene a meeting of principals of high schools and above, Director Jiao will visit the principals of various schools on a daily basis to exchange opinions.

Excellent Instructors: The association also believes that military instructors should reside in the school and manage the students' discipline at any time. Therefore, it strictly ordered the instructors of various schools to reside in the school, except for part-time instructors, and should sign in at the office and work on a daily basis, the same as ordinary instructors.

Liu Wendao Gives a Lecture at the Business School 31

Mr. Liu Wendao, the ambassador to Italy, was invited by the National Shanghai Business School to give a lecture at the school at 3:00 PM yesterday. All the teachers and students of the school attended. First, the dean of the school, Pei Fuheng, gave a welcome speech. Then, Ambassador Liu came to speak about the current situation in Italy. He first talked about the spirit of mutual assistance in the founding of Italy, and then explained in detail the actual situation in Italy's agriculture, industry, commerce, academic, and military aspects. Finally, he encouraged young people to work hard for the national rejuvenation movement. The lecture lasted for an hour and a half, and the audience was moved.

Municipal Library 33

Statistics on Reading and Borrowing Books for the Previous Month

7,941 Readers, 304 People Per Day

The Book Catalog of About 500 Pages Will Be Released Soon

Since Mr. Xu Zexiang became the director of the Municipal Library, he has added a circulation section, mobile library, and reading room, and purchased a large number of books.
